<h1 _ngcontent-lkk-c119="" class="doc-title ng-star-inserted" title="@ohos.inputMethodEngine (输入法服务)"> @ohos.inputMethodEngine (输入法服务) </h1>

<div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" auitextselectionexpansion="" class="markdown-body ng-star-inserted renderOptimization" style="position: relative;">   <div>    <p>本模块面向输入法应用（包括系统输入法应用、三方输入法应用），为输入法应用提供能力，包括：创建软键盘窗口、插入/删除字符、选中文本、监听物理键盘按键事件等。</p>    <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">      <p>本模块首批接口从API version 8开始支持。后续版本的新增接口，采用上角标单独标记接口的起始版本。</p>     </div></div></div>    <div class="tiledSection scroll-inwindow" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 247px;">     <h2 id="导入模块" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">导入模块<i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="导入模块" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><div </div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 658px;">     <h2 id="inputmethodenginegetinputmethodability9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputMethodEngine.getInputMethodAbility<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getInputMethodAbility(): InputMethodAbility</p>     <p>获取输入法应用客户端实例<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#inputmethodability">InputMethodAbility</a>，仅支持输入法应用调用。</p>     <p>输入法应用获取该实例后，可订阅软键盘显示/隐藏请求事件、创建/销毁输入法面板等。</p> id="mcps1.3.5.7.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#inputmethodability">InputMethodAbility</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入法应用客户端。</td>        </tr> <h2 id="inputmethodenginegetinputmethodenginedeprecated" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">inputMethodEngine.getInputMethodEngine<sup>(deprecated)</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="inputmethodenginegetinputmethodenginedeprecated" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>getInputMethodEngine(): InputMethodEngine</p>     <p>获取输入法应用客户端实例<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#inputmethodengine">InputMethodEngine</a>。</p>     <p>输入法应用获取该实例后，可订阅软键盘显示/隐藏请求事件等。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>从API version 8开始支持，API version 9开始废弃，建议使用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#inputmethodenginegetinputmethodability9">getInputMethodAbility()</a>替代。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.3.1.1" width="50%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.7.8.1.3.1.2" width="50%">说明</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#inputmethodengine">InputMethodEngine</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">输入法应用客户端。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1518px;">     <h3 id="createpanel10" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">createPanel<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="createpanel10" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>createPanel(ctx: BaseContext, info: PanelInfo, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;Panel&gt;): void</p>     <p>创建输入法面板，仅支持输入法应用在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethod-extension-ability#inputmethodextensionability">InputMethodExtensionAbility</a>类中调用。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>单个输入法应用仅允许创建一个<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#paneltype10">软键盘类型</a>和一个<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#paneltype10">状态栏类型</a>的面板。</p>       <p>输入法面板不支持创建子窗口。例如：不支持使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/application-window-fa#设置应用子窗口" target="_blank">window.createWindow</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-menu#bindcontextmenu8">bindContextMenu</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-methods-custom-dialog-box">CustomDialog</a>等接口创建子窗口弹窗。建议开发者采用非子窗的替代方案，如<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ohos-arkui-advanced-dialog">弹出框</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-menu#bindmenu">bindMenu</a>或设置showInSubwindow为false。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.36.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ctx</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inner-application-basecontext">BaseContext</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">createPanel<sup>10+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="createpanel10-1" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>createPanel(ctx: BaseContext, info: PanelInfo): Promise&lt;Panel&gt;</p>     <p>创建输入法面板，仅支持输入法应用在<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethod-extension-ability#inputmethodextensionability">InputMethodExtensionAbility</a>类中调用。使用promise异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>单个输入法应用仅允许创建一个<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#paneltype10">软键盘类型</a>和一个<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#paneltype10">状态栏类型</a>的面板。</p>       <p>输入法面板不支持创建子窗口。例如：不支持使用<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/application-window-fa#设置应用子窗口" target="_blank">window.createWindow</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-menu#bindcontextmenu8">bindContextMenu</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-methods-custom-dialog-box">CustomDialog</a>等接口创建子窗口弹窗。建议开发者采用非子窗的替代方案，如<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ohos-arkui-advanced-dialog">弹出框</a>、<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/ts-universal-attributes-menu#bindmenu">bindMenu</a>或设置showInSubwindow为false。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1669px;">     <h3 id="adjustpanelrect12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">adjustPanelRect<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="adjustpanelrect12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>adjustPanelRect(flag: PanelFlag, rect: PanelRect): void</p>     <p>预设置输入法应用横竖屏大小。接口调用完毕表示adjust请求已提交到输入法框架，不表示执行完毕。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">flag</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#panelflag10">PanelFlag</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">目标面板状态类型。类型为FLG_FIXED或FLG_FLOATING。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">rect</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#panelrect12">PanelRect</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">目标面板横屏状态及竖屏状态的横坐标，纵坐标，宽度以及高度。固定态：高度不能超过屏幕高度的70%，宽度不能超过屏幕宽度；悬浮态：高度不能超过屏幕高度，宽度不能超过屏幕宽度。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/errorcode-inputmethod-framework">输入法框架错误码</a>。</p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table class="tableClass2_t">                      <tbody><tr class="firstRow">         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.9.1.3.1.1" width="50%">错误码ID</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.68.9.1.3.1.2" width="50%">错误信息</th>        </tr><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">401</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">parameter error. Possible causes: 1. Mandatory parameters are left unspecified; 2. Incorrect parameter types; 3. Parameter verification failed.</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">12800013</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="50%">window manager service error.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-left"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-button expand-button"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">收起</div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div-header-right"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-button ai-button"></div><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-button line-button"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">自动换行</div></div><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-button theme-button"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">深色代码主题</div></div><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-button copy-button"><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="handle-hover-tips">复制</div></div></div></div><div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-scroll-div"><pre class="ts prettyprint linenums hljs language-typescript" data-highlighted="yes"><ol class="linenums"><li><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> { <span class="hljs-variable language_">window</span> } <span class="hljs-keyword">from</span> <span class="hljs-string">'@kit.ArkUI'</span>;</li><li>

style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1864px;">     <h3 id="adjustpanelrect15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">adjustPanelRect<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="adjustpanelrect15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>adjustPanelRect(flag: PanelFlag, rect: EnhancedPanelRect): void</p>     <p>预设置输入法应用横竖屏大小、位置、自定义避让区域以及热区。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>仅用于SOFT_KEYBOARD类型，状态为FLG_FIXED或FLG_FLOATING的面板。此接口兼容<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#adjustpanelrect12">adjustPanelRect</a>的调用方法，若入参rect仅填写属性landscapeRect和portraitRect，则默认调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#adjustpanelrect12">adjustPanelRect</a>。</p>       <p>此接口为同步接口，接口返回仅代表系统侧收到设置的请求，不代表已完成设置。</p>      </div></div></div> device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">on('sizeChange')<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onsizechange12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>on(type: 'sizeChange', callback: SizeChangeCallback): void</p>     <p>监听当前面板大小变化，使用callback异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>仅用于SOFT_KEYBOARD类型，状态为FLG_FIXED或FLG_FLOATING的面板。输入法通过adjustPanelRect等接口对面板大小进行调节时，系统会根据一定规则校验计算出最终的数值（例如超出屏幕等场景），输入法应用可通过该回调获取的真实面板大小，完成最终的面板布局刷新。</p>       <ul>        <li>从API version 12-14开始支持，此接口回调函数中仅包含<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/arkts-apis-window-i#size7">window.Size</a>类型的必选参数。</li>        <li>从API version 15起，调用<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#adjustpanelrect15">adjustPanelRect</a>接口后，此接口回调函数增加<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#keyboardarea15">KeyboardArea</a>类型的可选参数。</li>       </ul>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.73.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">type</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">监听当前面板的大小是否产生变化，固定值为'sizeChange'。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">callback</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#sizechangecallback15">SizeChangeCallback</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">回调函数。返回当前软键盘面板的大小，包含宽度和高度值。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setImmersiveEffect<sup>20+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <ul>        <li>当键盘拉起时设置常亮生效，键盘关闭则自动失效。</li>        <li>规范使用该接口：必要场景（例如：语音输入）下，设置该属性为true；退出必要场景后，重置该属性为false；其他场景下，不使用该接口。</li>       </ul> style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 346px;">     <h2 id="messagehandler15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">MessageHandler<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="messagehandler15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h2>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>自定义通信对象。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>开发者可通过注册此对象来接收已绑定当前输入法应用的编辑框应用所发送的自定义通信数据，接收到自定义通信数据时会触发此对象中<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onmessage15">onMessage</a>回调函数。</p>       <p>此对象全局唯一，多次注册仅保留最后一次注册的对象及有效性，并触发上一个已注册对象的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onterminated15">onTerminated</a>回调函数。</p>       <p>若取消注册全局已注册的对象时，会触发被取消对象中<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onterminated15">onTerminated</a>回调函数。</p>      </div></div></div>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1135px;">     <h3 id="onmessage15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">onMessage<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onmessage15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onMessage(msgId: string, msgParam?: ArrayBuffer): void</p>     <p>接收已绑定当前输入法应用的编辑框应用发送的自定义数据回调函数。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当已注册的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a>接收到来自已绑定当前输入法应用的编辑框应用所发送的自定义通信数据时，会触发该回调函数。</p>       <p>msgId为必选参数，msgParam为可选参数。存在收到仅有msgId自定义数据的可能，需与数据发送方确认自定义数据。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.97.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">msgId</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">接收到的自定义通信数据的标识符。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">msgParam</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">ArrayBuffer</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">接收到的自定义通信数据的消息体。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p> </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 883px;">     <h3 id="onterminated15" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">onTerminated<sup>15+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="onterminated15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>onTerminated(): void</p>     <p>监听对象终止回调函数。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>当应用注册新的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a>对象时，会触发上一个已注册<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a>对象的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#oninputstart9">on('inputStart')</a>获取到InputClient实例后，通过实例调用。</p>    </div>    <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1485px;">     <h3 id="sendkeyfunction9" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv" class="firsth2">sendKeyFunction<sup>9+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="sendkeyfunction9" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>sendKeyFunction(action:number, callback: AsyncCallback&lt;boolean&gt;): void</p>     <p>发送功能键。使用callback异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.100.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>输入法应用调用该接口向编辑框发送扩展编辑操作，编辑框监听相应事件<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethod#onhandleextendaction10">on('handleExtendAction')</a>，从而进一步做出处理。</p>       <p>编辑框响应<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#extendaction10">ExtendAction</a>的PASTE命令时，需要编辑框应用申请<a href="https://developer.huawei.com/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-guides/restricted-permissions#ohospermissionread_pasteboard" target="_blank">ohos.permission.READ_PASTEBOARD</a>权限。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.132.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.132.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">action</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1895px;">     <h3 id="setpreviewtext12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">setPreviewText<sup>12+</sup><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-device active" active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="setpreviewtext12" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>setPreviewText(text: string, range: Range): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>设置预上屏文本。使用promise异步回调。</p>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.136.6.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.136.6.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.136.6.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.136.6.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">text</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">string</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">将被预上屏的文本。</td>        </tr>        <tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">range</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#range10">Range</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">是</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>目标替换的文本范围。</p>          <p>- 当值为{ start: -1, end: -1 }时，默认将参数text替换当前预上屏区域全部文本。</p>          <p>- 当start等于end，默认将参数text插入start对应的光标位置。</p>          <p>- 当start不等于end，将参数text替换range对应区域的文本。</p>          <p>- 当start与end为其他含有负数值的组合，按照参数错误返回。</p>          <p>- 当输入框已有预上屏文本，参数range不得超过预上屏文本范围，否则按照参数错误返回。</p>          <p>- 当输入框无预上屏文本，参数range不得超过输入框文本范围，否则按照参数错误返回。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>返回值：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="cellrowborder" width="50%">无返回结果的Promise对象。</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>错误码：</strong></p>     <p>以下错误码的详细介绍请参见<a   <div class="tiledSection" style="contain-intrinsic-size: auto 1184px;">     <h3 id="finishtextpreview12" device-type="phone,2in1,tablet,wearable,tv">finishTextPreview<sup>12+</sup><i class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>sendMessage(msgId: string, msgParam?: ArrayBuffer): Promise&lt;void&gt;</p>     <p>发送自定义通信至已绑定当前输入法应用的编辑框应用。使用Promise异步回调。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p>该接口需要编辑框与输入法绑定并进入编辑状态，且输入法应用处于完整体验模式时才能调用。</p>       <p>msgId最大限制256B，msgParam最大限制128KB。</p> active-tips="隐藏支持设备" tips="显示支持设备"></i><i class="anchor-icon anchor-icon-link" anchorid="recvmessage15" tips="复制节点链接"></i></h3>          <div class="device-list active"><span class="support-device-pre">支持设备</span><span class="support-device-item">Phone</span><span class="support-device-item">PC/2in1</span><span class="support-device-item">Tablet</span><span class="support-device-item">TV</span><span class="support-device-item">Wearable</span></div><p>recvMessage(msgHandler?: MessageHandler): void;</p>     <p>注册或取消注册Messagehandler。</p>     <div><div class="hw-editor-tip info"><div class="title">说明</div><div class="content">       <p><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a>对象全局唯一，多次注册仅保留最后一次注册的对象及有效性，并触发上一个已注册对象的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onterminated15">onTerminated</a>回调函数。</p>       <p>未填写参数，则取消全局已注册的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a>，并会触发被取消注册对象中<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onterminated15">onTerminated</a>回调函数。</p>      </div></div></div>     <p><strong>系统能力：</strong> SystemCapability.MiscServices.InputMethodFramework</p>     <p><strong>参数：</strong></p>     <div class="tablenoborder">      <div class="tbBox"><table>       <thead>        <tr>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.141.7.1.5.1.1" width="25%">参数名</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.141.7.1.5.1.2" width="25%">类型</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.141.7.1.5.1.3" width="25%">必填</th>         <th align="left" class="cellrowborder" id="mcps1.3.141.7.1.5.1.4" width="25%">说明</th>        </tr>       </thead>               <tbody><tr>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">msgHandler</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%"><a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a></td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">否</td>         <td class="cellrowborder" width="25%">          <p>该对象将通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onmessage15">onMessage</a>接收来自已绑定当前输入法应用的编辑框应用所发送的自定义通信数据，并通过<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onterminated15">onTerminated</a>接收终止此对象订阅的消息。</p>          <p>若不填写此参数，则取消全局已注册的<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#messagehandler15">MessageHandler</a>对象，同时触发其<a href="/consumer/cn/doc/harmonyos-references/js-apis-inputmethodengine#onterminated15">onTerminated</a>回调函数。</p></td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div> Possible causes: 1. Incorrect parameter types.</td>        </tr>             </tbody></table></div>     </div>     <p><strong>示例：</strong></p>     <div _ngcontent-lkk-c106="" class="highlight-div"><div
